Keep original filename but prefix with ID for uniqueness\n        # Sanitize filename slightly to avoid issues, though discord.Attachment.filename should be reasonable\n        safe_filename = "".join(c if c.isalnum() or c in (\'.\', \'_\', \'-\') else \'_\' for c in attachment.filename)\n        save_path = self.temp_dir / f"{attachment.id}_{safe_filename}"\n        try:\n            await attachment.save(save_path) # discord.Attachment has a save method\n            self.logger.info(f"Successfully downloaded attachment using discord.Attachment.save: {save_path}")\n            return {\n                \'url\': attachment.url,\n                \'filename\': attachment.filename, # guild_id: Optional[int], channel_id: Optional[int], feature: str) -> bool:\n        """Check if a feature is enabled for a guild+channel combination.\n\n        Resolution: channel config > parent channel config > server default > False.\n        Requires guild to be enabled and write_enabled.\n        """\n        if guild_id is None:\n            return False\n\n        self._maybe_refresh()\n\n        feature_key = f"{feature}_enabled"  # e.g. \'logging_enabled\'\n\n        server = self._servers.get(guild_id)\n        if not server or not server.get(\'enabled\') or You can widen the search with a larger limit, different sort, specific channel, or days filter.
